***gebaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaar</a> (5620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebare</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebare</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebaren</a></i>. The sense “gesture” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> relatively recent and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> likely influenced by the sense “movement” and the related, now obsolete term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaarde.html>gebaarde</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>gesture <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of gesticulating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from early 18th c.]</span></li>
<li>gesture <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act or token of appreciation or lack thereof</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> movement, motion
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appearance

***gebeuren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a> (477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geburen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">geburien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen, occur</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaburjaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuren.html>beuren</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">geböhren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:barre.html>barre</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġebyrian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebieden.html>gebieden</a> (5772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebieden.html>gebieden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gebiodan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bieden.html>bieden</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebondenheid.html>gebondenheid</a> (61009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebonden.html>gebonden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebondenheid.html>gebondenheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebondenheid.html>gebondenheden</a></b>)

<li>connectedness</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedagen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">day</span> of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">person</span>'s <span class="Latn" lang="en">birth</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The Dutch language <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a distinction between the day of one's birth (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedag</a></i>) and the annual birth celebration day (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verjaardag.html>verjaardag</a></i>).
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gebroet</i>. ***gebruik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruik</a> (748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gebruuc</i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>use</li>
<li>custom, practice</li></ol>

***gebruiken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a> (448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gebruken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gibrūkan</i>. Equivalent to modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bruiken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consume, to eat or <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> (food or <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:consumeren.html>consumeren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nuttigen.html>nuttigen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consume (resources or goods)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:consumeren.html>consumeren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbruiken.html>verbruiken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
